To reduce contention\n45:   // on claiming array elements, worker threads claim parts of this array in chunks;\n46:   // Array elements may be null as threads might not get enough regions to fill\n47:   // up their chunks completely.\n48:   // Final sorting will remove them.\n49:   class G1BuildCandidateArray : public StackObj {\n50: \n51:     uint const _max_size;\n52:     uint const _chunk_size;\n53: \n54:     CandidateInfo* _data;\n55: \n56:     uint volatile _cur_claim_idx;\n57: \n58:     // Calculates the maximum array size that will be used.\n59:     static uint required_array_size(uint num_regions, uint chunk_size, uint num_workers) {\n60:       uint const max_waste = num_workers * chunk_size;\n61:       // The array should be aligned with respect to chunk_size.\n62:       uint const aligned_num_regions = ((num_regions + chunk_size - 1) / chunk_size) * chunk_size;\n63: \n64:       return aligned_num_regions + max_waste;\n65:     }\n66: \n67:   public:\n68:     G1BuildCandidateArray(uint max_num_regions, uint chunk_size, uint num_workers) :\n69:       _max_size(required_array_size(max_num_regions, chunk_size, num_workers)),\n70:       _chunk_size(chunk_size),\n71:       _data(NEW_C_HEAP_ARRAY(CandidateInfo, _max_size, mtGC)),\n72:       _cur_claim_idx(0) {\n73:       for (uint i = 0; i < _max_size; i++) {\n74:         _data[i] = CandidateInfo();\n75:       }\n76:     }\n77: \n78:     ~G1BuildCandidateArray() {\n79:       FREE_C_HEAP_ARRAY(CandidateInfo, _data);\n80:     }\n81: \n82:     // Claim a new chunk, returning its bounds [from, to[.\n83:     void claim_chunk(uint& from, uint& to) {\n84:       uint result = Atomic::add(&_cur_claim_idx, _chunk_size);\n85:       assert(_max_size > result - 1,\n86:              \"Array too small, is %u should be %u with chunk size %u.\",\n87:              _max_size, result, _chunk_size);\n88:       from = result - _chunk_size;\n89:       to = result;\n90:     }\n91: \n92:     // Set element in array.\n93:     void set(uint idx, G1HeapRegion* hr) {\n94:       assert(idx < _max_size, \"Index %u out of bounds %u\", idx, _max_size);\n95:       assert(_data[idx]._r == nullptr, \"Value must not have been set.\");\n96:       _data[idx] = CandidateInfo(hr);\n97:     }\n98: \n99:     void sort_by_reclaimable_bytes() {\n100:       if (_cur_claim_idx == 0) {\n101: ","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/jdk--742e735d@b394eab7f7a9ef928dbbcac1e27e0a0b1577894a/-/blob/src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CollectionSetChooser.cpp%3FL1-100"}}}
